 'loading': "Chargement...",
 'success': "Merci, vous recevrez prochainement nos offres spéciales !",
 'failure': "Vous êtes déjà inscrit à nos offres spéciales."
 };

 if (document.getElementById('emsnewsletter') !== null) {
 var nlForm_WP = document.getElementById('emsnewsletter'),
 nlStatus = document.createElement('div'),
 nlAction = nlForm_WP.action,
 btnAction = document.querySelector('.newsletter .btn');

 nlForm_WP.insertBefore(nlStatus, nlForm_WP.firstElementChild);

 // Listen for the form being submitted
 nlForm_WP.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
 e.preventDefault();

 btnAction.disabled = true;

 // Set up the AJAX request
 var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
 request.open('POST', nlAction, true);
 request.setRequestHeader('accept', 'application/json');

 // Create a new FormData object passing in the form's key value pairs (that was easy!)
 var formData = new FormData(nlForm_WP);

 // Send the formData
 request.send(formData);
 console.log(request);

 // Watch for changes to request.readyState and update the statusMessage accordingly
 request.onreadystatechange = function () {

 // < 4 = waiting on response from server
 if (request.readyState < 4) {
 nlStatus.innerHTML = nl_messages.loading;
 nlStatus.setAttribute('class', 'alert alert-info');
 }

 // 4 = Response from server has been completely loaded.
 else if (request.readyState === 4) {

 // 200 - 299 = successful
 if (request.status == 200 && request.status < 300) {
 nlStatus.setAttribute('class', 'alert alert-success');
 nlStatus.innerHTML = nl_messages.success;
 document.querySelector('.newsletter__form .input-group').style.display = "none";
 nlForm_WP.reset();
 } else {
 nlStatus.setAttribute('class', 'alert alert-danger');
 nlStatus.innerHTML = nl_messages.failure;
 }
 }
 }
 });
